operator flag
<FONT COLOR=MAROON>Not Connected, use /JOIN</FONT>
<FONT COLOR=PURPLE>Syntax: /IGNORE [-lr] &lt;nickname | !login | @domain | nickname!login@domain&gt;<BR>Block messages from certain users<BR></FONT>
Examples:
add all people with nick 'bob' to the ignore list
!bobl
add all people with login names 'bobl' to the ignore list
@bobd.com
add all people from the domain 'bobd.com' to the ignore list
bob!bobl@bobd.com
add a specific person to the ignore list
show ignore list entries
-r bob
remove an entry from the ignore list with nick as 'bob', login and domain not specified
-r !bobl
remove an entry from the ignore list with login as 'bobl', nick and domain not specified
-r @bobd.com
remove an entry from the ignore list with domain as 'bobd.com', nick and login not specified
-r bob!bobl@bobd.com
remove an entry from the ignore list with domain, nick and login specified
<FONT COLOR=PURPLE>Syntax: /ACTION &lt;action&gt;<BR>Shows the message as an action performed by you.<BR></FONT>
<FONT COLOR=PURPLE>Syntax: /AWAY [reply]<BR>Set/Clear automatic reply string for messages whispered to you.  /AWAY without a reply clears the message.<BR></FONT>
<FONT COLOR=PURPLE>Syntax: /BAN &lt;nickname&gt;<BR>Ban &lt;nickname&gt; from channel.<BR></FONT>
<FONT COLOR=PURPLE>Syntax: /BANLIST &lt;channel&gt;<BR>Show list of banned people for &lt;channel&gt;.<BR></FONT>
<FONT COLOR=PURPLE>Syntax: /DEOP &lt;nickname&gt;<BR>Remove OP privileges for &lt;nickname&gt;.<BR></FONT>
<FONT COLOR=PURPLE>Syntax: /IGNORE [-lr] &lt;nickname | address&gt;<BR>Ignore messages from &lt;nickname | address &gt;.<BR></FONT>
<FONT COLOR=PURPLE>Syntax: /INVITE &lt;nickname&gt;<BR>Invite &lt;nickname&gt; to the current channel.<BR></FONT>
<FONT COLOR=PURPLE>Syntax: /JOIN &lt;channel&gt; [key]<BR>Allows you to join a specific chat &lt;channel&gt;.<BR></FONT>
<FONT COLOR=PURPLE>Syntax: /KICK &lt;nickname&gt; [reason]<BR>Allows you to kick the user with the given &lt;nickname&gt; from the current channel.<BR></FONT>
<FONT COLOR=PURPLE>Syntax: /LEAVE<BR>Allows you to leave the current channel.<BR></FONT>
<FONT COLOR=PURPLE>Syntax: /LIST<BR>List all channels on server (may be very long).<BR></FONT>
<FONT COLOR=PURPLE>Syntax: /ME &lt;action&gt;<BR>Shows the message as an action performed by you.<BR></FONT>
<FONT COLOR=PURPLE>Syntax: /MSG &lt;nickname&gt;&lt;message&gt;<BR>Allows you to send a private message (whisper) to the person with that nickname<BR></FONT>
<FONT COLOR=PURPLE>Syntax: /NAMES &lt;channel&gt;<BR>Shows a list of who is currently active in the chat channel.<BR></FONT>
<FONT COLOR=PURPLE>Syntax: /NICK &lt;nickname&gt;<BR>Allows you to change your nickname display in the chat channel.<BR></FONT>
<FONT COLOR=PURPLE>Syntax: /OP &lt;nickname&gt;<BR>Give OP privileges to &lt;nickname&gt;.<BR></FONT>
<FONT COLOR=PURPLE>Syntax: /QUIT<BR>Quit chat, return to previous page.<BR></FONT>
<FONT COLOR=PURPLE>Syntax: /TOPIC [new topic]<BR>View or change the topic for the channel.<BR></FONT>
<FONT COLOR=PURPLE>Syntax: /UNBAN &lt;nickname&gt;<BR>Allow &lt;nickname&gt; into the channel.<BR></FONT>
<FONT COLOR=PURPLE>Syntax: /WHOIS &lt;nickname&gt;<BR>Display info for &lt;nickname&gt;.<BR></FONT>
<FONT COLOR=BLUE><B>No Channel</B></FONT>
